 function showPopUp(el) {
    var cvr = document.getElementById("cover");
    var dlg = document.getElementById(el);
    cvr.style.display = "block";
    dlg.style.display = "block";
    if (document.body.style.overflow = "hidden") {
       cvr.style.width = "1024";
       cvr.style.height = "100%";
    }
 }
 function closePopUp(el) {
    var cvr = document.getElementById("cover");
    var dlg = document.getElementById(el);
    if (cvr) { cvr.style.display = "none"; }
    if (dlg) { dlg.style.display = "none"; }
    document.body.style.overflowY = "auto";
 }

 function clearguns() {

    document.getElementById('bullets').style.background='white';
    document.getElementById('primers').style.border='2px dotted #d2e0ff';

 }

 function hidereloadingforms() {
    hidediv('bullets_form');   hidediv('primers_form');   hidediv('brass_form');   hidediv('powder_form');   hidediv('reloading_misc_form');}

                my: 'top',
                at: 'bottom',
                collision: "fit"
             }
          });
 
          jQuery(".switch").switchify();
       });
       </script>
